class=\"td-icon-whatsapp\"></i></a>\n</div></div>\n<div class=\"td-post-content\">\n<p><a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-37557\" src=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"828\" height=\"315\" srcset=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI.png 828w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI-150x57.png 150w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI-600x228.png 600w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI-768x292.png 768w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI-696x265.png 696w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI-120x46.png 120w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/Outliers-of-the-week-HI-500x190.png 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 828px) 100vw, 828px\"></a></p>\n<hr>\n<p>We come across a large number of interesting stocks in <a href=\"https://snap.capitalmind.in/#/outliers\" target=\"_blank\">Capitalmind SNAP Outliers</a>, our discovery tool for stocks with momentum. See a video of <a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/2015/03/premium-outliers-our-video-on-how-to-discover-stocks-using-the-tool/\" target=\"_blank\">how Outliers works</a>, and how to use Outliers to <a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/2017/03/premium-unlocked-how-to-find-stocks-hitting-all-time-highs-using-capitalmind-snap/\" target=\"_blank\">find all-time highs</a>. Here’s a stock we found interesting that’s been an outlier. Catch&nbsp;them all <a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/tag/outlier-in-focus/\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>.</p>\n<p>Today we take a look at&nbsp;<a href=\"https://snap.capitalmind.in/#/nse/STRTECH\" target=\"_blank\">Sterlite Technologies</a> [STRTECH]</p>\n<p>Headed by <strong>Anil Agarwal</strong>, STRTECH is a Telecom Solution Provider with wings spread across the globe coupled with manufacturing presence in China [optical fiber capacity of nearly 27 million fiber kilometres on an annualized run rate] and Brazil. STRTECH is engaged with key customers across Europe and partners global telecom operators in the Middle East, Latin America as well as Asian markets and European markets.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Logo.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-37581\" src=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Logo.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"230\" height=\"48\" srcset=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Logo.png 230w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Logo-150x31.png 150w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Logo-120x25.png 120w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 230px) 100vw, 230px\"></a></p>\n<p>With <strong>unprecedented opportunities surfacing in telecom industry</strong>, STRTECH demerged the power products and transmission business into a separate company called Sterlite Power Transmission last year. This helps STRTECH narrow its focus on the telecom space which is witnessing operator consolidations and spectrum wars.</p>\n<p>With the <strong>government’s Digital India program</strong> [STRTECH is working on the Smart Cities projects in Ahmedabad. , Gandhinagar and Jaipur. Some of the projects include <strong>10,000 km long fibre-based communication network intrusion-proof smarter data network</strong> for the Armed Forces, rural broadband for <strong>BharatNet</strong>, Smart Cities’ development, and establishing high-speed Fibre-to-the-Home (FTTH) networks] playing a major part in the future of the company.</p>\n<p>Adding more muscle power to its presence in the telecom industry, ST acquired a telecom software product company – <strong>Elitecore Technologies</strong> &nbsp;to increase its offerings to global customers in the form of software solutions for operations support, business support and revenue management.</p>\n<div class=\"td-a-rec td-a-rec-id-content_inline  \"><span class=\"td-adspot-title\">Get Capitalmind Premium</span><div class=\"td-all-devices\"><a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/get-capital-mind-premium/?utm_source=inline&amp;utm_medium=cmweb&amp;utm_campaign=Mar2007inline\"><img src=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2013/11/CM2017-Ad.jpg\" style=\"margin:10px\"></a></div><p>The stock as can be observed in the table below has been popping up in our <a href=\"https://snap.capitalmind.in/#/outliers\" target=\"_blank\">Outliers</a> table for quite some time and is currently trading at near its all time high.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Outlier-Info.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-37583\" src=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Outlier-Info.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"590\" height=\"373\" srcset=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Outlier-Info.png 590w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Outlier-Info-150x95.png 150w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Outlier-Info-120x76.png 120w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Outlier-Info-500x316.png 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 590px) 100vw, 590px\"></a></p>\n<h3>Financials last year</h3>\n<p>With the demerger having taken place, we look at the financials of the pure play telecom entity for last year alone coupled with information available as of April, 2017.</p>\n<ul>\n<li><strong>Net Revenue</strong> stood at Rs. 2,161 Crores in 2015-16 against the adjusted figure of Rs. 1,619 Crores in 2014-15.&nbsp;<strong>Export Revenue</strong> stood at Rs. 547 Crores in 2015-16 against the adjusted figure of Rs. 466 Crores in 2014-15.</li>\n<li><strong>Net Profit</strong> stood at Rs. 151 Crores in 2015-16 against the adjusted figure of Rs. 119 Crores in 2014-15.</li>\n<li><strong>Net Debt</strong> stood at Rs. 1,008 Crores in 2015-16 against the adjusted figure of Rs. 674 Crores in 2014-15 mostly on account of working capital finance, funding of capacity expansion projects in fibre and fibre cable business and acquisition of Elitecore.</li>\n<li><strong>Fibre Optic Sales</strong> volume stood at 6.5 million-fkm in 2015-16 against 7.8 million-fkm in 2014-15. [fkm stands for fibre kilo meters].</li>\n<li><strong>Revenue from Telecom Solutions and Services</strong> segment stood at Rs. 476 Crore in 2105-16 against the adjusted figure of Rs. 84 Crore in 2014-15.</li>\n</ul>\n<p><a href=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price.png\"><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-37582\" src=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"658\" height=\"525\" srcset=\"https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price.png 658w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price-150x120.png 150w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price-600x479.png 600w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price-526x420.png 526w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price-120x96.png 120w, https://capitalmind.in/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/ST-Share-Price-500x399.png 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 658px) 100vw, 658px\"></a></p>\n<h3>Financials 3Q</h3>\n<ul>\n<li>Mix between Software and Services stands at 22% and 77% of the Net Revenue.</li>\n<li>International Revenues have remained below 40% with <strong>contributions from China</strong> stands at close to 50% of the total export revenue [the company has 6-7% market share] <strong>China has a strong investment plan till 2019</strong> which includes fiber to the home roll outs as well as 5G roll outs.</li>\n<li><strong>Capex</strong> for the whole year was targeted at Rs. 220 crore and close to Rs. 160 crore has been utilized with the remaining amount expected to be consumed in Q4.</li>\n<li><strong>Net Debt as of Q3</strong> stood at Rs. 1,030 crore.</li>\n</ul>\n<h3>Current State</h3>\n<ul>\n<li><strong>Evolution of the usage of the internet</strong> with 2G primarily catering to the wide voice requirements evolving into 3G and now 4G in order to serve the high-speed data requirements of the customers along with voice.</li>\n<li><strong>Acceleration of connectivity requirements</strong> [quantum leap in technology clubbed with the increase in per capita data consumption] is raising the quantum of fiber deployment on a year-on-year basis.</li>\n</ul>\n<h3>Future Propsect</h3>\n<ul>\n<li>Base case estimate for <strong>fiber demand level for the year 2020 would be north of 500 million fiber kilometre</strong>. At current levels fiber production is using up most of the glass capacity globally.</li>\n<li>With <strong>roll over to 5G networks</strong>, look forward to further increase in fiber deployment as customer data requirements accelerate.</li>\n<li><strong>Ongoing OF capacity expansion</strong> program of 30 million fkm&nbsp;by September, 2017 from&nbsp;the current 27 million fkm.</li>\n</ul>\n<p>Connectivity, Content and Low Cost Smart Devices – are the three fundamental drivers that the company states are crucial for its growth.</p>\n<div class=\"linkwithin_hook\"
